I walked away and continued with my shopping, and I heard him chuckle as I walked off. When I came to p<span class="text_exposed_hide">...</span><span class="text_exposed_show">ay for my stuff up front I saw him trying to walk out the doors with like fifteen Milky Ways in his hands without paying.<br> The girl at the counter was very nice about it and professional, and was like Sir, you need to pay for those first. At first he kept pretending to be tired and not hear her, but eventually turned back around and brought them to the counter.<br> When she took one of the bars and started scanning it multiple times, he stopped her and told her to scan them each individually to prevent any electrical infetterence, and then turned around and winked at me. I dont even think thats a word.
